jeffhu@Jeffs-MBP: project$ python project.py
Welcome to the Ubiquitous Computing Machine (UCM), an automated decision system for stock picking.

This automated decision system recommends stocks to invest in on a given date based on only one signal:
1) The stock has to appear on that date on the 'Investing Ideas - Long Ideas' list on seekingalpha.com
2) The stock has to have appeared within 3 days on the same list

Then, the UCM will invest your money based on a number of methods:
1) 50 day moving average (same as hw2)
2) Buy and hold for the entire year
3) Trailing stop (15%)

Please enter the method you'd like to use:
1) for 50-Day Moving Average
2) for buy-and-hold
3) for trailing stop of 15%
Method: 2

Please enter 'backtest' if you'd like to see how the stocks that UCM picks
performs over the course of the next year. If you select this option, UCM
will randomly select 25 dates between 1 year ago and 2 years ago to invest,
and then backtest those stocks for the next year to see what the actual performance
would have been for your chosen method. Leave this blank to see yesterday's recommendations.
Backtest: backtest

You have chosen to backtest stocks that UCM picks. We'll compare the average return of each
portfolio and subtract from that the average return of the index to identify how much you beat
the market by with the given method and signal over the course of a year
